20/09/23, 17:38 - +91 62020 53648: *ECE Lab File Guidelines* 

i) On the index page, mention the Experiment name exactly same as what mentioned in the Syllabus.

ii) Stick/Append the Copy of Syllabus on the first page of File

iii) If there are multiple sub-experiments of the Experiment, no need to write objective, Apparatus and other parts seperately. Division between the two parts of the Experiments can be under the Sub-Headings wherever required, such as Observation, Results, etc

iv) Circuit Diagram drawn on left side should have all components drawn and labled. For example, LED or any extra thing used apart from the logic gates should also be mentioned. 

v) In diagrams showing the logic gate implementation, the input & output of every Gate should be labelled. 

vi) In the specification of the Apparatus/Devices/Components, the machine, Make and Model your group was using to perform the experiment should be mentioned. Example- If Power supply used is Keylight E 3682 , mention it. Now some other group may be using KeyLight E 3632 Model. So, mention accordingly.

vii) Date of Experiment should be mentioned atleast on the First Page of your experiment record apart from the Index Page

viii) Follow all instructions given by the Proffesor from time to time. <This message was edited>

13/01/25, 18:34 - +91 62020 53648: #include <stdio.h>

// Function to merge two subarrays
void merge(int arr[], int left, int mid, int right) {
    int n1 = mid - left + 1;  // Size of the left subarray
    int n2 = right - mid;     // Size of the right subarray

    // Create temporary arrays
    int leftArr[n1], rightArr[n2];

    // Copy data to temporary arrays
    for (int i = 0; i < n1; i++)
        leftArr[i] = arr[left + i];
    for (int j = 0; j < n2; j++)
        rightArr[j] = arr[mid + 1 + j];

    // Merge the temporary arrays back into arr[left..right]
    int i = 0, j = 0, k = left;
    while (i < n1 && j < n2) {
        if (leftArr[i] <= rightArr[j]) {
            arr[k] = leftArr[i];
            i++;
        } else {
            arr[k] = rightArr[j];
            j++;
        }
        k++;
    }

    // Copy remaining elements of leftArr[], if any
    while (i < n1) {
        arr[k] = leftArr[i];
        i++;
        k++;
    }

    // Copy remaining elements of rightArr[], if any
    while (j < n2) {
        arr[k] = rightArr[j];
        j++;
        k++;
    }
}

// Function to implement merge sort
void mergeSort(int arr[], int left, int right) {
    if (left < right) {
        int mid = left + (right - left) / 2;

        // Sort the first and second halves
        mergeSort(arr, left, mid);
        mergeSort(arr, mid + 1, right);

        // Merge the sorted halves
        merge(arr, left, mid, right);
    }
}

// Function to print an array
void printArray(int arr[], int size) {
    for (int i = 0; i < size; i++)
        printf("%d ", arr[i]);
    printf("\n");
}

// Main function
int main() {
    int arr[] = {38, 27, 43, 3, 9, 82, 10};
    int size = sizeof(arr) / sizeof(arr[0]);

    printf("Original array:\n");
    printArray(arr, size);

    mergeSort(arr, 0, size - 1);

    printf("Sorted array:\n");
    printArray(arr, size);

    return 0;
}
